    jQuery.fn.dataTableExt.oSort['title-asc'] = function (x, y) {
        var regex = /<a href="(\w.+)">(\w.+)<\/a>/;
        regex.exec(x);
        var x_comp = RegExp.$2;
        regex.exec(y);
        var y_comp = RegExp.$2;
        return ((x_comp < y_comp) ? -1 : ((x_comp > y_comp) ? 1 : 0));
    };

    jQuery(function ($) {

        function zebra() {
            $('#table1 tbody tr').removeClass('odd even');
            $('#table1 tbody tr:visible:odd').addClass('odd');
            $('#table1 tbody tr:visible:even').addClass('even');
        }

        function disable_grouping() {
            $('#table1 tbody tr').removeClass('hidden');
            $('#table1 tbody tr td a.group_parent').hide();
        }

        var oTable = $('#table1').dataTable({
            "oLanguage": {
                "sZeroRecords": "Keine Eintr&auml;ge vorhanden.",
            },
            "bPaginate": false,
            "bInfo": false,
            "bSortClasses": false,
            "bAutoWidth": false,
            "aaSorting": [],
            "fnDrawCallback": function () {
                zebra();
            },
            "aoColumns": [
                null,
                {"sType": 'title'},
                null,
                {"iDataSort": 3},
                {"bVisible": false}
            ]
        });
        $('#mybox').keyup(function () {
            disable_grouping();
            oTable.fnFilter($(this).val());
        })
        $('#table1 th.clickable').click(function () {
            disable_grouping();
            zebra();
        });
        $("#update_list").live("change", function () {
            var day = $(this).val();
            if (day != 0) {
                window.location = '/?stream_updates=' + $(this).val();
            }
            else {
                window.location = '/';
            }
        });

        $('.group_parent').click(function () {
            $('.group_' + $(this).attr('id')).show();
            $(this).remove();
            zebra();
        });
    });
